11.0pt;">前言：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span 11.0pt;">《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告》是维权网信息中心每月对大陆当下发生的羁押未判、强迫失踪和已经判刑的各个政治犯、良心犯案例予以汇总、统计，最终编辑和撰写了这一最新月度动态报告。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">自本月度报告的第<span lang="EN-US">101</span>期起，本报告全新改版。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">同时，鉴于</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">中国人权捍卫者（<span lang="EN-US">CHRD</span>）</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">所属的</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">《中国大陆良心犯数据库</span></b></span></span><a href="https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> </span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">已将本网月度报告中所涉及的良心犯均全部收录，因此，我们从<span lang="EN-US">101</span>期起，将绝大多数本月没有动态信息的良心犯简历不再在月度报告里显示。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">我们仍将把在押良心犯名录附于报告内，读者可以根据姓名登录进入《中国大陆良心犯数据库》</span></span></span><a href="https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/</span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">查询所有相关信息，非常便捷。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">《中国大陆良心犯数据库》不但收录了目前在押的这个良心犯、政治犯，已经获释、死亡的良心犯、政治犯也在此数据库中可以查询到。《中国大陆良心犯数据库》收集工作整理自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月开始，截止<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">09</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日共 收录良心犯资料共<span lang="EN-US">3469</span>人。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本报告主要关注的对象是所有在押的政治犯、良心犯——这里包括已被判刑的和羁押未判的——所有我们能够收集到确切信息的政治犯、良心犯。本报告竭力就包括汉、藏、维、哈萨克、回、蒙古、朝鲜、满等中国大陆多族裔政治犯、良心犯在内的信息进行收集、撰写和编辑，力求全面真实反映当前中国大陆政治犯、良心犯的恶劣的生存境遇。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告为了便于人们查询检索，完全以良心犯、政治犯的姓名拼音顺序制作了完整的在押人员名录。同时，本报告仍对所有良心犯、政治犯的刑期进行了统计，羁押未判的也全部列于最后。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告名单人员一旦取保候审、保外就医、无罪释放、回家监视居住、缓刑或刑满释放，都将从报告正式在押名单中移除，但其简历将显示于本期报告中。 <span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告每月不辍，期期更新，其中凝聚了许多义工、信息员和编辑长期以来默默无闻的辛劳和奉献。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">9</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年来，本网一共收集、整理、编辑过的有较为翔实资料的人员名单及其简历超过<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>多个<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">这个数字里内涵着本网所有工作人员在高度风险下的巨大付出。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告之所以能够按时定期发布，并且信息越来越翔实，这也得到了大陆许多人权捍卫者的积极反馈和支持。本网对所有提供信息的朋友，在此一并予以感谢。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">九年如一日，本网持续不断地对中国大陆政治犯、良心犯境况进行总结和报告，是为了抗议谴责中共当局以超期羁押、拖延审判、虐待折磨、殴打等各种方式对良心犯政治犯施加酷刑，而在中共狱中被酷刑虐待折磨是被关押者要经常面对的严酷现实。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本网坚信，外界坚持不懈的关注，将会给狱中受难者以精神和实质的援助！本报告一直对中共当局使用各种酷刑手段迫害折磨政治犯、良心犯的行径予以的系统揭露，业已引起了海内外各个方面的强烈反响。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网一直在及时更新、统计最新讯息，每月末发布这月度报告，谨以此表达我们对所有失去自由的政治犯、良心犯的关注和牵挂。并以此，告诉全世界不要忘记这些为自由、民主、人权而承担苦难的人们。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网认为，本报告的定期更新和发布，可以直接反映出大陆当下的人权概况——因为一个国家的政治犯、良心犯的境况是这个国家最重要的人权指标之一。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">以此</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">揭示中国大陆当下恶劣的人权概况与良心犯、政治犯的悲惨处境，力求唤起国际社会对中国在押政治犯、良心犯的记忆，并予以持续不断的关注和呼吁，直至他们获得自由。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网认为，定期将良心犯、政治犯的姓名和境况公诸于世，是我们能给予这些受难者以实际而有效支持的一种方式。我们深知，没有比被人们的遗忘更令这些良心犯、政治犯感到绝望和痛苦的事情。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">因此，我们必须肩负起这项工作，乃至是使命。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">八年多的风风雨雨已经过去，未来的道路上还会有千难万险，但是有你们的支持，我们仍将一如既往勇往直前！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">最后，本报告虽经本网信息中心认真核查，并得到中国大陆许多人权捍卫者协助，但仍因条件所限，无法做到适时、准确统计全部在押政治犯、良心犯信息，报告所反映的只是冰山之一角，仍然是一份不完全的报告，这需要我们的继续努力！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New class="MsoListParagraph" style="margin-left: 36.0pt; mso-char-indent-count: 0; mso-list: l14 level1 lfo24; text-indent: -36.0pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: 11.0pt;"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">一、<span style="font: 7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span></b><!--[endif]--><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本期报告概述：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告》月月更新，是一份关于中国在押政治犯、良心犯的动态报告。此为第<span lang="EN-US">108</span>期。至此，本报告月月发布历时已整整八年多。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本期报告全文共计</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">5</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">万<span lang="EN-US">8</span>千字</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">。本期报告对上期报告的所有政治犯、良心犯名单进行了一次全面的逐一核查。获悉上期名单中</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">60</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">人已被</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刑满释放或取保获释。并获悉有被羁押的<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人被判刑，<span lang="EN-US">10</span>人狱中有新动态，</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">同时，本期新增了我们又搜集的被刑事拘留和被精神病的<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人以及被判刑的<span lang="EN-US">38</span>人，合计<span lang="EN-US">47</span>人的名单及简介。目前，被本期报告录入姓名发布的在押良心犯、政治犯共</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1669</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">人。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">为便于人们查询，《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯名单索引》为本报告名单的唯一索引。索引是以姓名拼音顺序排列（<span lang="EN-US">ABCDEFG....WXYZ</span>）。同时，本报告对所有良心犯、政治犯的刑期进行了统计，羁押未判的也全部列于最后。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><a mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175727158;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span _Hlk175727158;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿旺益西：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175727158;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1984</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175727158;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，藏族名<span lang="EN-US">Ngawang Yeshe</span>，西藏自治区日喀则市人，日喀则市定日县协格尔镇查那村当卓寺（藏民称之为（<span lang="EN-US">Tengdro</span>）僧侣，公益慈善捐助人，藏族异见人士，良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-9</span>月，因当卓寺僧人曲嘉旺波（<span lang="EN-US">ChoegyalWangpo</span>）到西藏首府拉萨市做佛事访问时不甚将手机遗失在某咖啡馆，后被老板交予拉萨市警方处置；但因警方在查阅手机时，发现内存其及当卓寺众僧侣与尼泊尔同乡藏僧的聊天记录，尤其是存有<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月尼泊尔大地震时，他们向那里的藏民和寺院捐款赈灾等的信息记录，以及还存有和第<span lang="EN-US">14</span>世达赖喇嘛有关的照片及相关文献等；遂立即触碰到中共西藏当局的政治敏感神经，认定这是一起与境外敌对势力勾结，利用网络通讯对国家安全构成威胁的典型案件；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，其所在当卓寺突遭日喀则市当局派出的大批武警及公安警察袭击，所有僧人均被强迫接受政治洗脑教育数天，多人遭殴打；之后有<span lang="EN-US">20</span>名僧侣（含其在内）被刑拘，当卓寺及其附近的网络被切断；<span lang="EN-US">3</span>天后，除一名僧侣因向当局抗议而自杀，其余<span lang="EN-US">19</span>名僧人仍被羁押，数月不放；后其与曲嘉旺波等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>名藏僧均被日喀则市检察院以涉嫌“跟境外藏人联系、赈济尼泊尔地震，或拥有和达赖喇嘛有关照片或文献”为罪由予以批捕，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日获悉，其已被西藏自治区日喀则市中级法院以“危害国家安全罪”枉法判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月；其余三名僧侣亦被以同罪名分别重判<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-17</span>年不等。目前疑似在拉萨市札基监狱服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span _Hlk175727158;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175727158;"><span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生。河北省涞水县王村镇东王庄村人。一九九九年七月，中共发动对法轮功的残酷迫害后，老人曾两次被劳教：<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，被劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，时年<span lang="EN-US">66</span>岁的法轮功学员陈书义被警察入室抓捕。次日下午两点，陈书义被刑事拘留，被关押到涞水看守所至今。后获悉涿州市法院对陈书义秘密庭审，并判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。而他家人既没接到开庭通知，也没接到判决书。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175727158;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175727158;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175727158;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1963</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175727158;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月出生，山西省太原市杏花岭区人，广东省深圳市龙岗区居民，深圳达特计算机公司软件开发部经理，计算机软件专家，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。在深圳从业<span lang="EN-US">20</span>余年，曾任职于多家公司的软件部负责人，为人谦和儒雅，工作成绩卓越，尤其是在深圳达特计算机公司软件开发部担任经理时，曾参与过多项软件开发，且主持研发的掌上电脑“一指禅”及“蓝精灵数码词典”是当时优秀的高新技术产品；但因信仰、宣传法轮功，而遭中共深圳当局强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，突然被深圳市龙岗区警方从家中抓捕刑拘，并被送往深圳市龙岗区看守所关押，其家遭查抄；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被以涉嫌“邪教罪”转正式逮捕，指控其“系法轮功组织成员”，利用掌握的专业技术，组装伪基站给他人，并使用伪基站宣传法轮功，属违法行为；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，其案在深圳市龙岗区法院正式庭审，至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，被深圳市龙岗法院一审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，并罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；其不服上诉，后经深圳市中级人民法院二审裁决，依然维持原判，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。目前在广东省四会监狱服刑。</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">内蒙古赤峰市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">62</span>岁，是内蒙古赤峰市宁城县忙农镇三家村一位普通农妇，她因时法轮功学员而频遭当地中共人员骚扰迫害，于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年被迫离家漂泊，近年在河北廊坊居住。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，范美玲在廊坊市安次区租住屋被南门外派出所警察抓捕，关押到廊坊市看守所。随后遭批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日其被霸州市法院开庭，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元。范美令上诉至廊坊市中级法院，于<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被廊坊市中级法院驳回上诉，维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">9/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">冯少勇：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> 1971</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月出生，湖北省仙桃市张沟镇人，北京邮电大学博士，前北京邮电大学，广东省深圳市龙岗区长住居民，原深圳市某中学员工，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。早年曾在北京邮电大学读博士生，为人乐观谦和，人缘好，因是研究项目组技术骨干，曾于<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年在该校与同事成功研发机顶盒，并将个人所获奖金<span lang="EN-US">100</span>万全部捐给该校；但因信仰、宣传法轮功，遭中共北京当局严厉打压；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，其被深圳市龙岗区警方突然抓捕，次日被刑事拘留，并被送深圳市龙岗区看守所关押，其所在中学办公室、宿舍，其家及亲戚家当天均被查抄；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被以涉嫌“邪教罪”转正式逮捕，控其与另一法轮功友人陈泽奇“均系法轮功组织成员，二人利用掌握的专业知识，组装伪基站给他人，并使用伪基站宣传法轮功”，属于违法行为；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，其案件被深圳市龙岗区法院开庭受理，至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，其被深圳市龙岗法院一审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，并罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；其不服上诉，同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日经深圳市中级人民法院终审裁定，驳回上诉、维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。目前在广东省四会监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">10/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">盖里·奥斯曼（维）<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1980</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年代出生，新疆阿克苏地区柯坪县人，维吾尔族名<span lang="EN-US">HeytqaryOsman</span>，北京某高校阿拉伯语教师，伊斯兰教信徒，中国在押良心犯。早年，曾因工作需要，其和妻子艾敏汉·阿吾提双双一起到北京生活，并任教于北京某高校的阿拉伯语课程教学工作；自<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年起，因中共政府在新疆针对各少数族裔（尤指维吾尔族和哈萨克斯坦族等民族）开始推行“再教育营”的管控模式，以实现时任最高领导人习近平不断强化治疆政策的路线，故而再教育营规模不断扩大，直至<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，其规模达到高潮；此期间，因中共利用“再教育营”名目大批量非法扣押数以万计的维吾尔族、哈萨克斯坦族穆斯林，以及回族和少量的基督徒、外国公民（主指已移居哈萨克斯坦斯坦国并成为哈国正式公民），其等国内虽早已是中共治下的公职人员（或被国家批准认可）的维吾尔族穆斯林亦遭管控和严打；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-9</span>月，当其在北京高校放暑假返回新疆老家度假之时，突然被阿克苏地区柯坪县警方抓捕，涉罪不详；后其被阿克苏地区检察院以拒绝国家规定公职人员不信教、不进清真寺等相关宗教信仰保证书为罪由予以批捕，并最终被新疆阿克苏地区柯坪县法院一审以“与宗教相关”等罪名或以“拒签宗教信仰保证书”等罪名秘密重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年；其不服上诉，又经新疆阿克苏市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a 0pt;">郭远和：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">湖南省桂东县法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年代生，女，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年约<span lang="EN-US">70</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日上午，郭远和被桂东县<span lang="EN-US">610</span>李勇明带人，强行抢走她的袋子，其中有<span lang="EN-US">500</span>元现金和大法资料；随后<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被抄家，抢走家中所有的电脑、打印机、大量的现金、法轮功书籍等，家里的门被贴上封条。郭远和被关押在郴州看守所，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月份被庭审，被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。她现被关押在湖南省女子监狱高度戒备监区遭种种虐待，不让上厕所、侮辱谩骂、强制转化等折磨。她一度精神失常，被转入湖南省武警医院“治疗”，因灌食牙齿被撬掉<span lang="EN-US">8</span>颗，整个人瘦了一圈。<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/13/446156.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">海莱提•尼亚孜（维吾尔）：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1960</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，新疆维吾尔自治区塔城市人，原《新疆法制报》总编室主任、《法治纵横》杂志社副社长、《新疆经济报》前记者，原“维吾尔在线”网站的编辑和管理员以及维吾尔在线论坛版主，维吾尔著名媒体人，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，乌鲁木齐<span lang="EN-US">7</span>•<span lang="EN-US">5</span>事件后因多次接受包括香港《亚洲周刊》在内的采访，分析新疆骚乱的深层次原因，批评时任自治区书记王乐泉治理政策不当，并透露自己曾经在<span lang="EN-US">7.5 </span>前一天向新疆领导部门提出过预警却未被采纳等，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被警方从乌鲁木齐家中抓走，关押在乌鲁木齐天山看守所；<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日其家人收到当局的拘捕通知书，随后被乌鲁木齐法院以“危害国家安全罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年。现在新疆昌吉监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">14/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a name="_Hlk178339954"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">何善航</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2000</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年出生，香港油尖旺区人，香港理工大学毕业生，香港某国际知名公司职员，香港逃犯条例修订草案（民间和媒体俗称“送中条例”、“逃犯条例”或“引渡条例”）反对者，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>·<span lang="EN-US">1</span>尖沙咀抗议者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，因中共当局在香港推出“逃犯条例修订草案”，遭到香港民众普遍反对，遂掀起“反送中”运动，并由香港民间人权阵线发起「没有国庆，只有国殇」之游行，以期在庆祝中华人民共和国成立<span lang="EN-US">70</span>周年大会期间同步进行示威，由港岛铜锣湾游行至中环，向港府公开表达反对“逃犯条例修订草案”的要求，但却遭到香港警方的明确反对，并被公众集会及游行上诉委员会上诉后被驳回；熟料港府官方的这一反对立场和决定立即激怒了要求高度自治，“真普选”、“真自由”的香港民众的强烈反对，遂有大批民众决定自我承担法律后果，在<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日国庆节当天，在港多区自行发起“反对逃犯条例修订草案”示威抗议行动；何善航因支持“反送中”运动，故在此过程中亦积极参与了从尖沙嘴到油麻地一带的抗议示威，但因抗议过程中诸多香港民众与前来镇压的港警发生了严重的暴力冲突，遂遭港警的实弹打压，最终有多人被实弹打伤和被抓捕，其中，何善航等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人被以“参与暴力”之名强行拘捕；后其等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人被警方以“参与暴动”和“管有攻击性武器或管有物品意图损坏财产”等罪名提出指控，并将其案交于香港西九龙裁判法院进行聆讯庭审；后经多次提堂审理，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，其等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人“参与暴动案”终被西九龙裁判法院分别判处<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月至<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年不等刑期，其中，其被以“暴动罪”、“管有攻击性武器罪”等重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年；据悉，庭审中其父亲曾多次参与旁听，但后因被确诊为末期肺癌，或可很快离世，遂其辩护律师称其已得终身教训，希望法院能予轻判，然最终遭拒，仍维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。目前疑似在壁屋监狱（香港新界西贡区清水湾道<span lang="EN-US">397</span>号）服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/03/5.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">候井卫：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被当地派出所抓捕、抄家，不法人员抢劫走大法书、电脑笔记本上台、打印机<span lang="EN-US">4</span>台等本应该受法律保护的私人财物。其家人也被抓捕到派出所，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>天后家人被释放，但派出所派了一些村民监视侯井卫家人。侯井卫被关押在通州区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>侯井卫被通州法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b><span _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span 0pt;">河南信阳市法轮功学员。</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">家住信阳市浉河区，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年前开始修炼法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共集团开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，黄晓波向人们讲述法轮功被迫害的真相，被中共邪党抓捕、关押迫害，被迫害流离失所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，流离失所<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年多的黄晓波在信阳市潢川县巍岗乡讲真相时，遭不明真相的人构陷，被潢川县巍岗乡派出所抓捕，被关押在驻马店地区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年上半年，黄晓波被驻马店市驿城区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/1/%E6%B2%B3%E5%8D%97%E4%BF%A1%E9%98%B3%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E9%BB%84%E6%99%93%E6%B3%A2%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-440739.html"><span class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">景春：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1954</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日出生，吉林省盘石市人，吉林省盘石市安乐乡村民，维权冤民，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，曾因与同村另一村民发生的一次冲突而被警方于次年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日刑拘，并关押在盘石市公安局东山看守所，遭受严刑拷打；<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，被当地法院利用虚假证据，在未开庭的情况下，以“故意伤害罪”被判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，赔偿伤害人医药费<span lang="EN-US">1711.97</span>元；后经其妻刘金艳多次维权上诉，法院才不得不改判其无罪，并于<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日将其释放；获释后，因其就被枉法关押一年一案依法向法院提出国家赔偿申请，遭到法院无理拒绝，遂被迫走上漫长艰辛的维权之路，期间多次遭遇到地方当局的打击与迫害，身心俱损；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年底，因其再次向当地政府提出信访诉求，随被 盘石市警方于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日强行抓捕，并以涉嫌“敲诈勒索（政府）罪”被刑拘，关押于吉林省盘石市看守所；一个月后，又被以同罪名正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，被吉林省盘石市法院宣布重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，经二审裁决，驳回上诉，维持原判。目前在吉林省长春市宽城区兴业监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">云南昆明市法轮功学员。邝德英<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">21/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李谦：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，云南昆明法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年生，家住昆明市西山区白马干休所。因坚持修炼法轮功，李谦女士曾于<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日早上，因疑似派出所警察对她进行跟踪和监控，李谦只身来到昆明市棕树营派出所反映情况，并讲述法轮功被迫害真相，警察在送她出来的时候，李谦给了她几份法轮功真相资料，并嘱咐她退出邪党（党、团、队）组织才能保平安。结果被派出所警察抓捕抄家。关押在昆明市看守所。后<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日李谦即被昆明市西山区公安分局逮捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被昆明市西山区法院秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并处罚金一万元人民币。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被送到云南省第二女子监狱关押。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span 0pt;">：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年开始修炼法轮功，李霜因传播法轮功真相，曾两次被绑架、关押，一次被判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，李霜曾被上海市金山区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被伊春市公安局伊美分局国保大队、西城派出所警察押回当地关押，后被伊春市友好区检察院起诉到友好区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，李霜被伊春市友好区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US">1946</span>年生。北京大学退休高级工程师、法轮功学员。一九九六年开始修炼法轮功，一九九九年七月中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，李占金多次遭中共迫害，被非法拘留、强制“洗脑”，被非法劳教、非法判刑。李占金于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日上午被北京市海淀区公安分局、燕园派出所张艳辉等七个警察闯入家中抓捕、抄家。后李占金老人一直被非法关押在海淀区看守所。被绑架关押构陷近两年，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日被海淀法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1947</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年已<span lang="EN-US">76</span>岁。农民，家住江苏省昆山市玉山镇。<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年，昆山市就有多名法轮功学员被上门骚扰，并有多名法轮功学员被抓捕，关进了派出所或看守所。当时由于疫情关系，派出所或看守所拒收，凌秀英就是其中之一。后警方突然通知凌秀英被判一年四个月，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，凌秀英被抓捕到苏州第四看守所。三天后，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，<span lang="EN-US">76</span>岁的凌秀英被劫持到江苏镇江女子监狱（未成年人管教所）迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"> _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江省北安市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日夜晚，马义涛等三名法轮功学员开车到五大连池市发放法轮功真相资料。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日凌晨，他们被跟踪的警察抓捕，同时被抓捕的法轮功学员还有李学良、盛春霞。随后警察驱车到北安市城区马义涛的家抄家，抢劫走几本大法著作和真相资料，并抓捕了马义涛的妻子马英杰。）<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，马义涛等四人被黑龙江省亚布力林区法院判刑。马义涛被判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，李学良<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，马英杰<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，盛春霞判三年缓四年，已回家。马义涛、李学良不服法院非法判决，提出上诉。马义涛刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; name="_Hlk178340734"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span 0pt;">2022</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年四十多岁，是沈阳市第六医院的护士。王荣军、那艳母女俩于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日左右失踪。亲朋好友到处寻找，从那艳工作单位，到派出所，到街道，没有任何人提供讯息。直到<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，亲属才得到母女俩被绑架并被判刑的确切消息。现在她们仍被非法关押在沈阳市第一看守所。王荣军及女儿那艳已分别被辽中区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月。刑期到：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/22/443930.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，宋宇岑在沈阳医大一院向病人讲法轮功真相，与人分享走出忧郁症的秘诀，遭护士恶告，被保安带到保安室并报警。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，宋宇岑被沈阳市和平公安分局警察关入和平区看守所。被抓捕、关押近两年，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日家属得知他被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年生，黑龙江省伊春市法轮功<span style="mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">五营区学员。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功，孙德香遭中共邪党人员抓捕、关押，<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日曾经被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月初，孙德香被伊春市公安局恶警秘密抓捕。孙德香后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，现已被关押在黑龙江省女子监狱。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月获悉孙德香现在身体被迫害得很严重，被转到黑龙江省监狱管理局中心医院，说是肠癌，家属被告知交钱并签字，是给孙德香做手术。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月初。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孙桂昌</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林省德惠市五台乡法轮功学员。孙桂昌和肖永芬夫妇各被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，已经于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月份被羁押到公主岭监狱和吉林省女子监狱。孙桂昌和妻子肖永芬<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被不法警察入室绑架。孙贵昌被送到德惠市拘留所非法拘留五天。肖永芬被送到长春第二看守所检查身体，不合格拒收，第二天下午<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点多钟放回家，被监视居住。后来，孙桂昌被非法关押德惠看守所。肖永芬因身体和精神状况被放回家，并被监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日左右，吉林省公安厅数个警察将在其女儿看家的肖永芬绑架。据悉，肖永芬以前在长春黑嘴子劳教所被迫害得精神失常，现在患有高血压和糖尿病（后期），脚部严重溃烂，现在被关押在吉林省女子监狱八监区；孙桂昌被关押在公主岭监狱九监区。多年来，上述两个监狱公开执法犯法，利用死人床、坐小板凳、长期剥夺睡眠、电棍电击、殴打、上绳等各种酷刑残害和转化善良无辜的法轮功学员，多人被迫害致伤、致残、致疯、致死。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">孙晶：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">又名孙静，女，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日出生于丹东，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年开始修炼法轮功的学员，家住抚顺市将军地区。孙晶的丈夫胡国舰因为修炼法轮功，曾两遭冤狱，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，被中共迫害致死。孙晶深受刺激，心身疲惫，健康出现危机。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年，她有缘开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，孙晶和王秀国，因在抚顺市顺城区前甸镇附近给民众介“法轮功，被顺城区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，各被罚金五千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/28/458206.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; Roman&quot;;">吉林省松原市干安县法轮功学员。家住松原市干安县唱子村，在中共对法轮功的疯狂迫害中，孙占国曾连续两次被非法劳教，曾被关押在吉林省九台饮马河劳教所，遭受酷刑虐待。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被干安县油田采油厂派出所抓捕，被关押一年后，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被干安县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。王君洲在天津市滨海新区生态城当保安，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日（或<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日）下班时，被滨新区生态城分局警察抓捕，据说是因为在微信中转发香港反送中相关信息。在王君洲被关押<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多后，被天津市滨海新区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日王梅英被广州市海珠区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年七十二岁；女儿那艳四十多岁，是沈阳市第六医院的护士。王荣军、那艳母女俩于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日左右失踪。亲朋好友到处寻找，从那艳工作单位，到派出所，到街道，没有任何人提供讯息。直到<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，亲属才得到母女俩被绑架并被判刑的确切消息。现在她们仍被非法关押在沈阳市第一看守所。王荣军及女儿那艳（那燕）已分别被辽中区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月。刑期到：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被惠民县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，王秀国和孙晶，因在抚顺市顺城区前甸镇附近给民众介“法轮功，被顺城区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，各被罚金五千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日下午对依兰县、佳木斯市桦川县两地法轮功学员实施绑架，到<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日共有<span lang="EN-US">29</span>人被绑架，其中十四名法轮功学员宋玉芝、施凤香、施凤兰、王云杰、周妍、邓术梅、宋孔华、武桂琴、卜宝玲、夏桂华、唐立飞、姚怀英、康艳玲、庞秀贤，与薛宏亮（未修炼法轮功）被长期关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日遭依兰县法院庭审。王云杰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江省哈尔滨市法轮功学员，女。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日下午，哈尔滨市香坊区魏淑杰在香坊区旭升南街海富山水文园小区发法轮功资料时，被举报，被香坊分局建筑街派出所抓捕。后魏淑杰被所谓的“取保候审”回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，魏淑杰外出买菜回来，在楼道里被抓捕，她被关进哈尔滨第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日上午九点，黑龙江省哈尔滨市道外区法院在没有通知家属、律师的情况下，对法轮功学员魏淑杰女士进行视频开庭。魏淑杰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。魏淑杰关押在黑龙江省女子监狱服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/19/450936.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span Roman&quot;;">肖永芬：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林省德惠市五台乡法轮功学员。孙桂昌和肖永芬夫妇各被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，已经于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月份被羁押到公主岭监狱和吉林省女子监狱。孙桂昌和妻子肖永芬<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被不法警察入室绑架。孙贵昌被送到德惠市拘留所非法拘留五天。肖永芬被送到长春第二看守所检查身体，不合格拒收，第二天下午<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点多钟放回家，被监视居住。后来，孙桂昌被非法关押德惠看守所。肖永芬因身体和精神状况被放回家，并被监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日左右，吉林省公安厅数个警察将在其女儿看家的肖永芬绑架。据悉，肖永芬以前在长春黑嘴子劳教所被迫害得精神失常，现在患有高血压和糖尿病（后期），脚部严重溃烂，现在被关押在吉林省女子监狱八监区；孙桂昌被关押在公主岭监狱九监区。多年来，上述两个监狱公开执法犯法，利用死人床、坐小板凳、长期剥夺睡眠、电棍电击、殴打、上绳等各种酷刑残害和转化善良无辜的法轮功学员，多人被迫害致伤、致残、致疯、致死。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">熊起亮</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江肇东市法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1978</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，黑龙江省肇东市警察抓捕了二十多名法轮功学员。据悉，此次绑架有黑龙江省公安厅介入，警察在两、三个月前就开始对法轮功学员进行跟踪、蹲坑。有的法轮功学员当天被放回，有的被非法拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天。其中占祥军、袁爱荣、杨淑君、孙琴、熊起亮<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人被关押、刑事拘留、批捕起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被黑龙江省安达法院开庭，<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被宣判：熊起亮被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，并罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月开始修炼法轮大法，身心受益。后曾三次在洗脑班、两次在精神病院被关押迫害，一次被非法劳教二年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张霞、张秀玲、邢果花（现年<span lang="EN-US">75</span>岁）三人都是张家口市张北县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日下午三点多，张北县国保大队四个警察（便衣），以调查一些事为由，在张霞家楼下强制张霞戴手铐绑架；五点多以同样的手段绑架了法轮功学员邢果花；六点多又绑架了法轮功学员张秀玲。随后讲他们关押到张家口看守所关押；<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被到张北县检察院；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被构陷到张北县法院。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被张北县法院秘密判刑，张霞<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚款三万元；张秀玲<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款两万元，邢果花<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚款两万元。张霞向张家口中级法院上诉。邢果花、张秀玲已经于<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被转入到石家庄女子监狱迫害。张秀玲刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: lang="EN-US">51</span>岁，原是密山市农电局下属厂的工人。其早年修炼法轮功。中共当局于一九九九年七月二十日开始发动迫害，赵波因坚持修炼法轮功而屡遭迫害。赵波于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月下旬被密山市国保警察抓捕、刑拘，之后被所谓“取保候审”；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月再次被警察抓捕，关押在密山看守所，八个月后被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。期间家属不能探视、没被通知开庭，也没见判决书。目前赵波已经被关押到泰来监狱，狱方也不让家人探视。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US">9</span>日在长春市火车站失踪后一直下落不明，她女儿多方寻找也不知道人在何处。后获悉，赵淑琴老人已遭中共法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被关押在位于长春市的吉林省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年底开始修炼法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功，朱海燕多次被抓捕、被关押、劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年、判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，朱海燕等<span lang="EN-US">14</span>名法轮功学员被银川市永宁县公安局恶警抓捕、抄家，朱海燕被关押在银川市看守所，后被银川市永宁县公安局构陷到银川市西夏区检察院；遭银川市永宁县公安局和银川市西夏区检察院相互勾结迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被银川市西夏区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生。金美华因坚持信仰法轮功，曾于<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被中共抓捕，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，中共法庭再次开庭，对金美华，在<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年的判刑的基础上，又加刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，共<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年。金美华一直在浙江女子监狱中遭受迫害。获释后，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日早上，警察去金美华家又对其抓捕并抄家，而后，金美华被关押在杭州市女子看守所。随后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，西湖区法院下达判决，金美华被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，罚金三万；目前，金美华被关押在浙江省女子监狱入监队。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">74</span>岁，辽宁地矿测绘院的退休职工，家住沈阳市沈北新区。早年修炼法轮功，在中共对法轮功迫害的二十五年中，亷晶坚持修炼，曾被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半和判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。廉晶老先生<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，被沈阳市公安局铁西分局警察抓捕；后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月初获悉，廉晶被当地法院判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款五千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span bold;">早年因为其哥哥在一起交通事故中被撞死亡，法院帮助大连市港务局逃避法律责任而上访维权。在其维权过程中，盛兰福积极参与各种公民活动，对当局打压维权律师行为进行公开批评。为了打压盛兰福，当局在几年时间内对盛兰福给予了二十多次的行政拘留，还有四次刑事拘留，被北京公安带走失联更是象家常便饭。对此，盛兰福曾经开玩笑说要申请被拘留的吉尼斯纪录。除此之外，其还多次遭到当局关押其进精神病医院的非法迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日获悉，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月下旬盛兰福遭北京公安局房山分局构陷妨碍公务罪被刑事拘留，现关押在北京房山看守所。盛兰福本次拘留是因为起诉北京公安机关多次非法配合当地抓捕，案件程序到法院开庭审理期间，盛兰福在法院论理却被法院构陷妨碍公务罪拘留，由北京公安局房山分局派出所在<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日将盛兰福抓捕入狱。后取保获释。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年出生，美籍华人，英文名<span lang="EN-US">David Lin</span>，美国爱荷华州（<span lang="EN-US">Iowa</span>）和加利福尼亚州（<span lang="EN-US">California</span>）经济顾问，基督徒，美国基督复临安息日会牧师，中国家庭教会宣教士，良心犯。自移民美国以来，早期曾专注于养家糊口，并自己熟知的领域一直努力工作；后入籍成为美国公民，曾在爱荷华州和加利福尼亚州担任政府官员的经济顾问；来美之初，其并无基督信仰，并认为只有无知的人才会信教，但多年之后，当其妻子成为基督徒后，其开始深入了解基督教信仰；后其受洗成为基督徒，并自此开始积极参与教会的服事活动；<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代，因其经常到中国旅行，期间深感基督教福音在中国广传的必要性，遂立定心志，以期能从中国官方最终获得开始基督教事工的许可；<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年，已是教会牧师的他开始了中国大陆宣教之旅；此期间，因中国政府为成功申办<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年奥运会，曾一度营造“外松”形象，故一时吸引了众多基督教工作者来华宣导，但实因中共本质上的思想意识倾向与基督教宣传的价值取向完全相左，遂在<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年前后启动的一项代号为“台风五号”秘密行动中，数以百计的外国来华传教士被驱逐；其亦在此打压行动中；<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年，林大卫牧师因帮助中国家庭教会盖一座教堂而被中国警方突然拘押和被禁止离境；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，林大卫被中国某检察院以所谓涉嫌“合同诈骗罪”予以批捕，指控其因“合同欺诈”而触犯了中国相关法律，故而应予逮捕、重判；随后其案很快被检察院起诉，并将其案宗移交至中国某法院审查；同年，终被中国某法院以“合同诈骗罪”枉法重判无期徒刑；据悉，被判之初，其家人尚选择保持沉默和低调处事，因其表明已将监狱视为施教、分享信仰和鼓励来自<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多个国家的囚犯的机会，故其在狱中建立了每周一次的礼拜天祷告会，并致力于将圣经译成中文；后至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-2019</span>年初，其在与家人的定期电话中突然明确要求帮助其尽早获得释放；后从官方得知其健康状况正在恶化，疑指可能“遭非人道虐待”等，遂开始寻求美国拜登总统及政府的帮助，以期能被早日无罪释放；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月获悉，其已被中共当局执行减刑，但刑期仍需至<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日获悉，林大卫先生在遭中共当局羁押<span lang="EN-US">18</span>年后日前终于获释，已经回到美国。</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">59/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a name="_Hlk178429807"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1980</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日出生，湖南省株洲市人，人称“小彪”，湖南省宁乡市黑金时代小区居民，人权捍卫者，“公民运动”践行者，中国在押政治犯。近年来，曾因积极参与公民维权活动，经常发布被中共当局打压的公民行动者的第一手信息，随遭湖南省当局的维稳监控；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月及<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，曾因为公开声援许志永和常玮平等良心犯而被当地警方传唤；同年，曾因声援香港反送中运动，并在香港著名媒体大亨、社会活动家黎智英被抓捕后，公开表态支持黎智英及香港《苹果日报》，而遭湖南警方多次警告，并被威胁、暗示当局正在搜寻对其实施抓捕的证据；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，因关注并协助曾于<span lang="EN-US">2018 </span>年在上海街头向习近平肖像泼墨而被“维稳”（即被当局非法关进精神病医院）的“泼墨女孩”董瑶琼，在推特上发求救呼吁，随立遭当局的严厉打压，被湖南省株洲市芦淞区警方从在宁乡市的家中带走传唤；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，被以“寻衅滋事”罪由处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天，其家被查抄；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，又被株洲市芦淞区警方以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”转为指定居所监视居住；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被芦淞区警方以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”转为刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，又被株洲市芦淞区检察院以同罪名予以批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其案在湖南省株洲市监管中心内宣判，欧彪峰获刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。一直被羁押于株洲市公安局监管中心看守所。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日后其微信朋友圈停止更新，两部手机均打不通，后确认被王官庄派出所以辱骂国家领导人为由刑事拘留。后被正式逮捕，关押在山东省济南市（长青区）第三看守所。后获悉，济南公民顾聪因言获罪于<span
