mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">三、本期获悉狱中<span lang="EN-US">12</span>人的动态信息（附简历）<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></a></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">11</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年：</span></b></span></span></span></span><a name="_Hlk178508729"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">上官云开</span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刑期不明：</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">吕华、</span></span></span></span></span><a name="_Hlk162565472"></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><a name="_Hlk170538828"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1/</span></b></a></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">上官云开：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">一审获刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年的湖北反腐记者<a name="_Hlk178473339">上官云开</a>案二审改判为<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，已转监黄石监狱服刑<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">（维权网信息中心报道）<a name="_Hlk178473463"><span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，本网获悉：湖北反腐记者上官云开案二审被鄂州市中级法院改判为有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">34</span>万元，据悉，二审在<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月份作出判决。现如今，上官云开已经被押赴黄石监狱服刑。</a><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">上官云开简介：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">著名反腐记者。<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日生于湖北荆门，祖籍广东梅县，属于客家人。曾担任《法治日报》驻湖北记者站站长，著有《让弱者哭出声》、《珠海的爱与痛》等书，在其创作生涯当中，曾使近<span lang="EN-US">300</span>名官员、黑恶分子受到处理。他是于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日从澳大利亚返国，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日上午突然与外界失去联系，现已证实上官云开已被湖北鄂州市公安局以涉嫌销售假药罪刑事拘留，目前羁押在鄂州市第一看守所。律师会见遭拒。而李庆亮律师发视频解读了著名反腐斗士上官云开记者因涉嫌销售假药罪被刑事拘留一案，他认为本案是司法机关选择报复性执法。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，资深反腐记者上官云开被湖北鄂州市鄂城区法院判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，据悉，判决属于数罪并罚，包括销售假药、寻衅滋事、诈骗、非法拘禁和重婚<span lang="EN-US">5</span>项罪名，合并判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年的同时，还罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">38</span>万元。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日获悉：湖北反腐记者上官云开案二审被鄂州市中级法院改判为有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">34</span>万元，据悉，二审在<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月份作出判决。现今，上官云开已经被押赴黄石监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/1511.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span lang="EN-US" Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/1511.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吕华：“湖北新视点网”负责人吕华被秘密判刑，官方刻意封锁消息刑期不明<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，本网获悉：据知情人透露，<a name="_Hlk178473763">吕华于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年年初被法院判处有期徒刑十年以上，但是该消息尚未得到官方和家人证实。据了解，因为吕华案被海外媒体高度关注，当地司法机关除了在判决之前发布了相关信息之外，公检法三家均对判决结果守口如瓶，以防止舆论发酵。</a><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吕华简介：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">湖北黄冈自媒体“湖北新视点网”负责人。男，<span lang="EN-US">1984</span>年生。湖北新视点网捆绑的公司为湖北新视点文化传媒有限公司，法定代表人是吕华，工商系统显示，吕华旗下还有多家公司，其亲任法人代表。包括商务咨询以及房地产经纪等。吕华失联数月，近日，据知情人透露，吕华已于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月中旬被黄冈市公安局抓捕。其经营的自媒体最后一次发布停留在<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，其后便不再更新，而黄冈市公安局曾于<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日通过官方网站公开征集吕华犯罪线索。由此推断，其遭抓捕的时间应该在<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日或<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。据了解，吕华经营的湖北新视点网曝光尺度较大，曝光了一些列黄冈当地的事件，包括女子发抖音被拘留、医护人员在<span lang="EN-US">CT</span>室内进行飞线充电等，还持续关注丰县铁链女遭遇。最引起巨大震动的当推曝光团风县大数据局女局长陈莉公款打造高档午休房一事，该消息被国内众多主流媒体跟进报道。后，在湖北新视点网站上的原报道均已删除。据知情人透露，吕华在被抓捕之前，与资深反腐记者上官云开多有互动，目前尚不清楚吕华的涉嫌罪名为何。吕华于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年年初被法院判处有期徒刑十年以上，但是该消息尚未得到官方和家人证实。据了解，因为吕华案被海外媒体高度关注，当地司法机关除了在判决之前发布了相关信息之外，公检法三家均对判决结果守口如瓶，以防止舆论发酵。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">贾榀简介：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">南方街头运动人士、河南籍民主人士。贾榀曾在<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年因言获罪遭广东警方以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，后获释。据悉，贾榀在二十大前去往广西北海市，随后向友人传信说被河南国保带回，从<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日至今再无消息。至今已经超过<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，目前处于强迫失踪的状态。<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/2_26.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/2_26.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">季孝龙：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月的上海著名人权捍卫者季孝龙狱中情况通报<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，本网获悉：上海著名人权捍卫者季孝龙因在疫情期间发声，向时任上海市委书记李强发出实名请愿书，要求其下台并承担重大事故责任，而被当局以“寻衅滋事罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。季孝龙自今年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日从上海新收犯监狱转监到提篮桥监狱，开始正式服刑，至今已两个月，但他的家属仍然无法会见他<span lang="EN-US">.</span>通过多方查询，季孝龙应该关押在上海提篮桥监狱<span lang="EN-US">11</span>监区，并处于单独关押状态。季孝龙在上次坐牢（<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>—<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日刑满）出狱后查出多种疾病，尤其需要急切处理的牙齿问题。在本次入狱开庭（<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日）的时候还没有得到治疗，而移送到监狱后家属更是无法了解季孝龙的任何情况。他的家庭对他目前狱中处境无能为力，需要国际上加大力度给予关注。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">季孝龙简介：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1976</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日出生，江苏省张家港市人，张家港市杨舍镇名都花苑居民，基督徒，民主人士，人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，曾因宣传民主理念而被上海市浦东新区警方以“寻衅滋事”罪由传唤，并被处以行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，曾因在网上发文，呼吁民主人士响应“厕所革命”，并在医院、大学等公共场所的厕所门上，用马克笔写宣传语“大病治不起，习胖狂撒币，修宪妄称帝、苦难何时毕！打倒共产党。还政于民，结束民众苦难。推翻习核心，拒走文革路”等字句，短时间内响应者众多，随于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被浦东新区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，又被送到指定居所监视居住；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，被以同罪由转正式逮捕，关押在上海市浦东新区看守所。 羁押期间，警方曾多次以让其“死亡”和用寒冷气温逼迫其认罪，致其身体虚弱发病吐血；其家属曾送羽绒服和《圣经》书籍遭拒收。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其案被上海市浦东新区检察院起诉至上海市浦东新区法院；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，最终被该法院以“寻衅滋事罪”一审判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。后送上海市白茅岭监狱七监区服刑，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日刑满获释。服刑期间遭到虐待。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年季孝龙出狱时正值疫情。在当年上海封城期间，其为上海市民持续发声，在互联网上公开发表《速停运动式防疫，纾困解难发救济》请命书，要求当局停止运动式防疫措施，向时任上海市委书记、现任总理的李强进行实名问责，要求其下台并承担重大事故责任。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，再次被上海市梅园新村派出所警察从家中带走，后被上海市浦东新区警方以“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，被浦东新区检察院以同罪名正式批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，季孝龙一审被以寻衅滋事罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，公诉方以他在推特上公开批评国家领导人作为罪证。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月二审秘密开庭，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月上海市第一中级法院终审维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年，季孝龙获得当年度的“青年中国人权奖”。季孝龙目前服刑于上海市提篮桥监狱，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/462024925.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/462024925.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">3/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">何方美：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">律师会见何方美情况通报：何方美坚持要求对女儿应有的赔偿和补偿，法院不同意，家人仍不知两个女儿下落<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，本网获悉：日前，张科科律师到河南省新乡市看守所会见了何方美。何方美坚持要求对女儿应有的赔偿和补偿，法院不同意。法院置母亲为女儿维权索赔和行政问责于不顾，一直关押不放！家人至今不知两个年幼女儿的下落和处境。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，何方美的辩护律师介入后，才知何方美的案件一审已经开过庭，但办案单位未通知何方美亲属；李新已被判刑五年，在河南焦作监狱服刑；其子被辉县市政府送至村民家里寄养；两幼女继续被关在共济医院。律师向辉县市法院主张阅卷和重新开庭，均被拒绝。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月开始，何方美家属去共济医院还能偶尔探视俩女孩。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年夏天，俩女孩被关进有电子锁的病区，家人们无法正常探视，只能通过护工偶尔获知女孩近况，辗转送物资。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，律师向新乡市中级人民法院提出控告，才于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月获许阅卷。目前，该案一审开庭两年多，迟迟未判<span lang="EN-US">38</span>岁的母亲何方美非常担心孩子们的生活、身心健康情况、受教育状况，希望早日出来照顾、陪伴孩子。她和李新的儿子被政府安排寄养村民家，两个女儿——<span lang="EN-US">7</span>岁的希希（化名）和<span lang="EN-US">3</span>岁的娇娇（化名）——也于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年清明节前被转移至它处，目前下落不明。亲属非常担忧两个小女孩的安全。我们严厉谴责河南省新乡市辉县市政府及辉县市公检法，他们应对何方美一家的残酷迫害承担直接责任！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">何方美简介：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1985</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日出生，河南省新乡市辉县人，网名“十三妹”，“疫苗宝宝之家”维权团体发起人，人权捍卫者，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年度“曹顺利人权捍卫者奖共同获得者，中国在押维权人士。自<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日其年仅<span lang="EN-US">1</span>岁<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月龄的小女打了百白破疫苗之后导致全身瘫痪，其多方求助投诉均被拒，遂逐级维权讨说法，后因多地亦发生类似疫苗伤害宝宝事件，随组建“疫苗宝宝之家”维权团体共同呼吁，以求当局关注并给予合理赔偿救治；然当局却对此一拖再拖，其被迫到北京上访，故屡遭抓捕打击；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，因中共两会期间与各地问题疫苗家长到北京王府井为残儿募捐，随被新乡市辉县警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，又被以辉县警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”转刑拘，关押在河南省新乡市看守所；因期间一直拒绝认罪，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被新乡市辉县检察院以同罪名批捕，后被起诉并罗列<span lang="EN-US">6</span>项罪，建议量刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其案在河南省辉县法院正式开庭；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，又被辉县检察院以“事实不清、证据不足”为由撤诉，后被无罪获释；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，因其不断发声请求国家立法解决疫苗问题、呼吁联合国关注中国疫苗问题等，而在北京再度遭遇强迫失踪；释放后，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，因当地政府阻挠其带疫苗致残的女儿看病，随对辉县政府招牌泼墨抗议，而被行政拘留；后于<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日第二次对辉县市政府泼漆抗议；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，知其及其丈夫、六岁的儿子、三岁的残疾女儿一起被警方软禁，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，其被河南省辉县市警方以涉嫌“重婚罪”和“寻衅滋事罪”正式逮捕；据悉，羁押期间，其产下一女，有关部门已致电其家属，称若不去领回孩子，其所有孩子将被送到福利院。目前被羁押于河南省新乡市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，河南辉县警察骗遭软禁的何方美说快要放她了，带她出去拍照体检，结果第二天直接把何方美带去参加庭审。她被当庭逮捕。其亲属接到逮捕通知后立刻聘请了律师。可律师来辉县法院时，法院以案件已经开过庭，审判委员会已经讨论过了为由，拒绝律师阅卷。辉县法院连律师阅卷都不准许，本案谈何公正处理？何方美多年来致力于疫苗群体维权。其实她自己也有听力残障，即天生没有耳廓、耳洞，需要大声或者看唇语来跟别人交流。本案在辉县法院开庭时，法院只让她听审，拒绝她看任何书面材料。她当庭才知丈夫李新被以寻衅滋事罪、重婚罪判了<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年多，已在服刑中。何在开庭时解除了法援律师，提交了<span lang="EN-US">50</span>页的自辩词。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/blog-post_25.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/blog-post_25.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">4/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">伊力哈木·土赫提<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">维吾尔族学者<a name="_Hlk178475307">伊力哈木·土赫提</a>被中共当局判处无期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>周年 请大家签署大赦国际发起的请愿书，敦促中共当局立即无罪释放伊力哈木·土赫！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，本网获悉：十年前的<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，维吾尔族学者伊力哈木·土赫提被中共当局以分裂国家罪判处无期徒刑；他于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被捕，至今已被监禁超过<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月。伊力哈木·土赫提先生倡导民族间的理解与对话，却被中共当局以分裂国家罪被判处无期徒刑。请大家签署大赦国际发起的请愿书，敦促中共当局立即无罪释放伊力哈木·土赫！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"></span></span></span><a href="https://amnesty.org/en/petition/china-must-end-decade-of-injustice/"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://amnesty.org/en/petition/china-must-end-decade-of-injustice/</span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">伊力哈木</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑;"> </span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 楷体;">土赫提简历：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1969</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区阿图什人，原中央民族大学维吾尔族教师，维族学者，维汉双语网站“维吾尔在线”创建人，中国在押政治犯。曾于<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年创办维吾尔在线网站，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年新疆乌鲁木齐发生“<span lang="EN-US">75</span>”事件期间，因该网站被当局视为进行了“大肆煽动宣传，传播谣言”的活动，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，伊力哈木及其家人即被中共当局带走，隔离软禁于北京周边某处，后来在作家王力雄等数百人联署的《关于维吾尔学者伊力哈木</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 楷体;">土赫提遭拘押的呼吁》之下，</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">8</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，才被释放回家；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，又因北京发生天安门撞桥事件，遂于<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日在开车带孩子及妻子外出时遭遇国保便衣警察的驾车冲撞及恐吓。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，再次被北京及新疆警察从家中带走刑拘，被羁押于新疆自治区公安厅看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，被乌鲁木齐市检察院以涉嫌“分裂国家罪”正式批捕，理由是“伊力哈木</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 楷体;">土赫提与境外‘东突’势力勾结”，利用互联网鼓吹‘新疆独立’，利用讲堂煽动</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">'</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">推翻政府<span lang="EN-US">'</span>，利用教师身份从事分裂活动”；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，最终被新疆自治区中级法院以“分裂国家罪”重判无期徒刑，没收个人全部财产；其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日二审再次宣判：驳回上诉，维持原判；据悉，其亲属前往送钱及衣服等物品时遭狱方拒绝，理由是伊力哈木的钱尚未用完，被羁押者无需送衣物。目前在新疆自治区第一监狱服刑（乌鲁木齐市新市区四平路<span lang="EN-US">5</span>号，邮编<span lang="EN-US">830013</span>）<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/10_23.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/10_23.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> </span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">5/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张海涛：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">获刑<span lang="EN-US">19</span>年的新疆人权捍卫者张海涛狱中长期遭酷刑折磨妻子恐其生命不保<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，本网获悉：李爱杰（新疆张海涛妻）今通报：“张海涛因言获罪，为争取人权获刑<span lang="EN-US">19</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，海涛姐姐到新疆沙雅监狱会见到了他，姐姐多方奔走求助，时隔快<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年才于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>视频会见了海涛，姐姐说：“当他出现在屏幕时，我惊呆了，不是在特定环意下，我已经认不出他就是日夜思念的弟弟，看到他面色苍白，皮包骨头，完全失去了原有的样貌。张海涛姐姐从未放弃过努力，经历了多少次被踢皮球和推诿。时隔一年，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日下午，张海涛从监狱给姐姐打过来一个电话，通话时长<span lang="EN-US">5</span>分钟。主要问了我和孩子在美国的情况，姐姐说他声音听起来依旧沉稳坚定。张海涛<span lang="EN-US">19</span>年刑期漫长，他被单独关押在一个四面封闭，只留一个小窗口的囚室。限制其与家人通话、写信，不让消费，不允许家属会见。如果不及时解除酷刑虐待，他将生命不保。恳请各位朋友继续关注、支持张海涛！下面是通讯地址：新疆<span lang="EN-US">15</span>号信箱<span lang="EN-US">9</span>分箱，请大家给他写信或寄明信片，感谢大家！”<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张海涛简历：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1971</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，河南省南阳市镇平县籍人，原<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代国企下岗工人，新疆区域电信产品销售者、自由职业者，权利运动义工，人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年，因其从所在国有企业被迫下岗，随前往新疆谋生，并从事电信产品零售业；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，曾在河南省南阳市老家渡假时突遭无辜抓捕，并被新疆警方以涉嫌“诈骗罪”刑拘，关押在乌鲁木齐市六道湾看守所；后关押近<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月后，又被无罪、无说法地释放；为了维护个人合法权益，其开始接触中国的司法公正问题；近几年，又因积极关注新疆民族问题和民生事务，热心协助访民维权，经常在网上发表对政府和时局的看法及不同意见，并参与权利运动网站的义工活动等；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，曾参与《要求立即撤销国务院<span lang="EN-US">&lt;</span>关于劳动教养问题的决定<span lang="EN-US">&gt;</span>等劳教行政法规的公民权力主张书》的签名活动；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，曾因六四<span lang="EN-US">25</span>周年纪念而遭到当地警方的拘禁、讯问。基于其以上长期的民主维权言行，遂引起中共当局的强烈不满和仇视；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被新疆维吾尔族自治区乌鲁木齐市中亚南路派出所警方以涉嫌“煽动民族仇恨、民族歧视罪”抄家、刑拘，其家中银行卡全部被冻结；<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，又被变更罪名以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，再次被变更罪名以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”继续超期关押；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，被新疆维吾尔族自治区乌鲁木齐中级法院以“煽动颠覆国家罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，以“为境外提供情报罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，二罪合并执行<span lang="EN-US">19</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并处没收个人财产人民币<span lang="EN-US">12</span>万；其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，经新疆维吾尔族自治区高级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2034</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日；据悉，其在看守所和狱中长期遭酷刑虐待、歧视及不平等待遇等；如在看守所时，给同囚室犯人发食物而不给他发，睡觉时故意放着空床位不睡却让两个犯人把他挟在中间挤着睡，一审判决书后一直让其戴沉重脚镣，从<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日起一直没有放过风；狱中，曾连续<span lang="EN-US">20</span>天日夜不让睡觉不准闭眼，如困了就用打火机在其头前后左右点着烧，不给食物和水，时常遭辱骂、威胁、恐吓、欺骗，夜间经常被拉到无监控器的地方及地下室蒙头用手拷反吊着打，拳打脚踢和用空心胶管、蝇子拍殴打头部、胳膊、腿等部位，白天被审问。目前在新疆维吾尔族自治区沙雅监狱九监区服刑，通讯地址：新疆<span lang="EN-US">15</span>号信箱<span lang="EN-US">9</span>分箱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/19_19.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/19_19.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">6/7/</span></b></span></span></span><a name="_Hlk178476200"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黄雪琴、王建兵</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">关注组：雪饼案三周年声明——我们要继续发声<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2024</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，广东省高级人民法院（下称广东高院）罔顾新的证据和线索，不经审讯，秘密签发“雪饼案”二审（终审）判决书，驳回雪饼两人上诉，维持一审不公判决。雪饼两人代理律师共四人（其中王建兵代理律师萧云强辩护资格被高院刻意忽略）直到<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日晚间才突然得知二审已被秘密宣判，此前未收到任何法院通知和文件，雪饼两人自辩权和律师辩护权均被变相剥夺。二审（终审）的突袭性秘密宣判，正是雪饼两人三年来所遭遇的公安违法办案和司法程序不公的极端写照，也是中国政府压制外界舆论的经典策略。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黄雪琴简介：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1988</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年生，女权人士、独立记者，曾任《新快报》及《南都周刊》的调查记者，关注性别、平权、官员贪污、企业污染、弱势群体等议题，也参与多起<span lang="EN-US">#MeToo</span>案件的报道和为性侵害性骚扰受害人提供帮助和支持。黄雪琴本计划于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年赴香港大学就读法学硕士，但后于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被广州警方以“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，后改指定居所监视居住至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日取保获释。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年，黄成功获得英国志奋领奖学金支持，原计划于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日前往萨塞克斯大学（<span lang="EN-US">Universityof Sussex</span>）就读发展学硕士。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日黄雪琴遭广州警方抓捕，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日开庭审理，未当庭宣判。黄雪琴、王建兵“煽动颠覆国家政权”案<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日上午在广州市中级人民法院开庭宣判，一审判决黄雪琴有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、王建兵有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。黄雪琴当庭表示要上诉。一审判决书如下：被告人黄雪琴犯煽动颠覆国家政权罪，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并处沒收个人财产人民币十万元。刑期自判决执行之日起计算。判决执行以前先行羁押的，羁押一日抵折刑期一日，即自<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日起至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日止。目前羁押在广州市第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王建兵简介：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1983</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日生，甘肃省天水市人，化名“煎饼”，独立公益人，北京西部阳光基金会前农村教育项目主管，广州恭明社会组织发展中心前青少年成长项目主管和残障社群赋能项目统筹，职业病工人权益倡导者，法律知识指导服务者，中国大陆<span lang="EN-US">#MeToo</span>运动重要支持者，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年大学毕业以来，热心从事公益事业<span lang="EN-US">16</span>年，故朋友及认识他的人都喜叫其“煎饼”；曾积极加入北京西部阳光农村发展基金从事农村发展工作，并担任该基金会农村教育项目主管<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年；曾为开启长期关注青少年教育及成长的公益职业生涯，而于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年加入广州恭明社会组织发展中心，担任青少年成长项目和残障社群赋能项目主管及统筹，支持和发起相关小区项目工作；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年起，开始关注职业病工人权益倡导及服务性工作，并提供必要的法律支持，同年，为关注和支持中国妇女人权活动，而成为中国大陆<span lang="EN-US">#MeToo</span>运动中重要的支持者；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日王建兵、黄雪琴遭广州警方抓捕，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日开庭审理，未当庭宣判。黄雪琴、王建兵“煽动颠覆国家政权”案<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日上午在广州市中级人民法院开庭宣判，一审判决黄雪琴有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、王建兵有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。黄雪琴当庭表示要上诉。一审判决书如下：被告人王建兵犯煽动颠覆国家政权罪，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，剥夺政治权利年，并处沒收个人财产人民币五万元刑期自判决执行之日起计算。判决执行以前先行羁押的，羁押一日抵折刑期一日，即自<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日起至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日止。目前被羁押于广州市第一看守所（广东省广州市白云区后岗北街第一看守所，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">510430</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/blog-post_21.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/blog-post_21.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">8/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黄琦：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">获刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年的著名人权捍卫者黄琦的<span lang="EN-US">90</span>多岁老母亲蒲文清身体仍然持续恶化 母子会见权利没有任何保障<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，本网获悉：获刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年的著名人权捍卫者、年已<span lang="EN-US">61</span>岁的黄琦先生的<span lang="EN-US">90</span>多岁母亲蒲文清的身体仍然持续恶化，与此同时，母子俩的会见权力没有得到任何保障。他母亲仍然处于<span lang="EN-US"> 24 </span>小时监控之中。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><a name="_Hlk178476440"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黄琦</span></b></a></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">简历：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1963</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日出生，四川省内江市人 “六四天网”网站创办人、中国天网人权事务中心负责人，人权捍卫者，中国在押良心犯。因长期关注社会热点话题，<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年曾成立“天网寻人事务所”，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年曾设立“六四天网”网站，并惯于在网上发表时政敏感性文章，从而累遭当局严控、传唤、刑拘和判刑；曾因言获罪，先后三次遭到警方的拘捕，且前两次都被判刑；<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，曾因国外异议人士在其网页上发表有关<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年天安门事件的文章，而被四川成都警方刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被正式逮捕，<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被四川省成都市中级法院以“煽动颠覆国家政权”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年；狱中曾遭法警、狱警和其他罪犯多次毒打，导致脑积水，脑萎缩，双侧脑室扩大，导水管变窄等严重疾病；出狱后，<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，曾改组六四天网为中国天网人权事务中心，创办了中国大陆第一家综合性人权组织，同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日荣获第六届中国人权青年奖；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，曾因发表有关四川地震灾难问政府的报导（即网上发文揭露汶川地震出现的“豆腐渣”工程），而第二次被成都市警方刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被正式逮捕，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被成都市武侯区法院以“非法持有国家秘密罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，<span lang="EN-US"> 2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日刑满释放；然而此时因在狱中长期遭受煎熬和非人待遇，已罹患肾脏绝症；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，因对一份内部文件内容曝光，其第三次被四川省绵阳市警方从成都家中带走刑事拘留，自此失联，同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被以“为境外非法泄露国家机密罪”正式逮捕，并被关押在绵阳看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月初，其案被移交四川绵阳市法院审理；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，被四川省绵阳市法院一审以“故意泄露国家秘密罪”、“为境外非法提供国家秘密罪”共判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年；其不服上诉，后经绵阳市中级人民法院二审裁决，依然维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。目前被在四川省巴中监狱服刑。据悉，黄琦狱中曾遭虐待迫害，常被犯人殴打致腿部受伤，家人所寄存款亦被狱警随意扣押；身体健康极差，有肾功能衰竭危险，患脑积水、心脏病、肺气肿和肺炎等多种严重疾患。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/1290.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/1290.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">9/</span></b></span></span></span><a name="_Hlk178476733"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">谢阳</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李国蓓律师：谢阳案庭前会议，律师抗议审判长违法主持，被迫休庭！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李贵生律师自<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月向长沙中院寄送委托手续后，承办法官余丹在长达<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个多月的时间内没有向李贵生律师送达起诉书，并在<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日召开庭前会议时称从现在开始确认李贵生律师有辩护人资格，立即遭到辩护人的强烈反对。余丹法官继续埋头往下推进其他事项，辩护人强烈抗议回避事项未处理前余丹法官没有资格继续主持庭前会议！<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日<span lang="EN-US">14</span>：<span lang="EN-US">10</span>，庭前会议被迫结束！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">谢阳简历：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1972</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日出生，湖南省长沙市人，天地人律师事务所和长沙京盈科律师事务所前任律师，原湖南纲维律师事务所律师，人权律师，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年正式执业以来，曾因代理多起公权力滥权案件，如山东省曲阜县薛明凯案、北京新公民运动张宝成案、河南省南乐县南乐教案、湖南省浏阳市张开华征地案等维权案件，并积极关注和参与社会维权运动（包括探访盲人律师陈光诚和声援建三江被捕律师等），而屡遭司法当局阻扰和逼迫打压；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，曾因只身前往山东省东师古村探望盲人律师陈光陈，而被地方黑恶势力殴打抢劫；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，曾因代理一起民间借贷纠纷案，为维护当事人利益要求取得合议庭商议结果，而被湖南省律师协会罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元，并被所在事务所要求解除合同和离职；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，曾因为“山东薛家命案”作委托代理律师，而被湖南省司法厅当局带走“约谈喝茶”；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，曾因为代理湖南省浏阳市土地维权者张开华案，在出庭时遭到当地法院的野蛮阻扰；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，因多次代理维权案件，而遭到湖南省律师协会变相打压，不予批准转所手续；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，因其积极代理多起长沙市雨花区强制征地拆迁案件，在代理莲湖村农民征地行政诉讼时，曾遭到当地法院非法驱逐；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，因其代理广西南宁北部湾建材市场当事人的维权案件，曾遭到多名不明身份人员的持械群殴，致其重伤，右腿骨折，其虽报警，但当地警方却迟迟不予出警；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，其在中共“<span lang="EN-US">709</span>大逮捕”中被湖南省长沙市警方抓走，后被以涉嫌“扰乱法庭秩序”、“煽动颠覆国家政权”二罪指定地点监视居住，代理律师要求会见遭拒；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，被长沙市警方以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，其案在湖南省长沙中级法院开庭受审，但因其被迫当庭认罪，否认曾受酷刑，遂于当日暂获取保候审；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被长沙市中级法院正式宣判：犯煽动颠覆国家政权罪，但免予刑事处罚；后其虽未被判刑入狱，但仍遭长期软禁和贴身监控；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，谢阳因<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年末前往湖南省永顺县声援因发表网络言论而被强制关进精神病院的怀孕女教师李田田，遂被长沙市警方带走失联，后知被以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”、“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；其住处遭查抄，许多个人物品均被损毁，两台计算机及一个保险柜被搜走；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被长沙市检察院以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”予以正式批捕。狱中遭酷刑。目前谢阳律师被羁押于长沙市第一看守所（湖南省长沙市长沙县泉塘街道远大二<span lang="EN-US">1736</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">410131</span>）。</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/08/27.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/08/27.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/blog-post_3.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/blog-post_3.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">10/</span></b></span></span></span><a name="_Hlk178477704"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阮晓寰</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（编程随想）：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">一审获刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年的网络工程师阮晓寰（编程随想）案二审进展情况通报：本人及律师均要求二审依法公开开庭审理上海高院再次申请了二审延期（<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日）<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，本网获悉：一审获刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年的网络工程师阮晓寰（网名编程随想）案二审的进展情况，现在通报如下： 阮晓寰妻子昨发文：“这一个多月，张冬硕律师来上海阅卷、会见了阮晓寰多次。基于一审的种种问题，阮晓寰本人、张律师和莫律师都分别于<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月初上书高院，要求二审依法公开开庭审理！律师也<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月第二周向上海高院递交了辩护意见书。张律师刚确认，上海高院再次申请了二审延期（审理至<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月底审结）。”阮晓寰妻子此前表示：对一审的枉法判决，对二审违法程序问题，现应依法澄清和追究。二审必须依法公正公开！尽快结束法治地狱般闹剧！其二审被中共当局刻意拖延，从<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日立案至今已<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。过去的一年多，高院承办须法官用法援律师占位，阮本人和家属不断要求废法援律师用自聘律师，其不做任何应答，导致阮晓寰合法权益被剥夺，长期羁押与外界彻底隔绝。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阮晓寰简介：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">网名“编程随想”。<span lang="EN-US">1977</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日出生，福建省泉州市人，上海市杨浦区民京路<span lang="EN-US">558</span>号长住居民，网络安全工程师，民主异见人士，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月间，曾因撰写含有针对中共当局及其政体制度等不利信息的文章百余篇，并将其发布于境外网络平台，在引发网民广泛热议的同时；也引起了中共官方的高度警惕、极端不满和伺机打击；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，因其曾经常使用网名“编程随想”，被中共国安人员查出其在豆瓣网注册过用的个人信息（内含大量针对中共政权的批评性言论），遂被上海市杨浦区警方从家中带走，次日即被以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘，家遭查抄，当场搜走正在使用中的计算机、手机及多部<span lang="EN-US">/</span>件私人电子设备等物品；同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被上海市杨浦区检察院以同罪名正式批捕，指控其因长期存有对中共政权的不满情绪，多次“使用计算机编写<span lang="EN-US">100</span>多篇带有造谣、诽谤煽颠性文章，内容涉及攻击抹黑现行政治体制、煽动颠覆国家政权、意图推翻社会主义制度”，并通过境外网站进行发布，造成大量网民浏览、评论、转发和效仿等“恶劣后果”，因而触犯了国家相关法律，应当逮捕法办；在被严重超押近<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，终被上海市第二中级法院一审以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”秘密重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，没收财产人民币<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日；其不服，上诉；据悉，其被宣判后，其父兄两家均遭警方约谈施压，“劝”其听任政府为其聘用律师，其妻亦遭警察围堵训诫<span lang="EN-US">2</span>小时；截至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，同月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日其案已被上海市高级法院立案，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，鉴于上海高级法院率先在二审期间使用“法援”律师侵占辩护席位，导致其妻委托律师无法行使合法辩护权，故其家人对相关司法人员的渎职行为和侵犯被告人辩护权等要求彻查纠正。目前阮晓寰被羁押于上海市杨浦区看守所（上海市杨浦区中原路<span lang="EN-US">1101</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">200438</span>）。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/7-2024927.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/7-2024927.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> </span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"></span><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><a name="_Hlk175883967"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四、</span></b></a></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">本期新增被刑事拘留及被精神病的<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人名单及简历<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">：</span><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><a name="_Hlk175805580"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">葛志慧、高兟、张文鹏、朱桂芹、白才明、李旭芳、张展、覃律、华秀珍<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></a></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175805580;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175805580;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">葛志慧：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年出生，北京市丰台区人，丰台区魏家村南<span lang="EN-US">20</span>号院公民，维权残疾人士，实名举报人，人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年，其商业用房曾遭政府暴力强拆，财产被洗劫一空，并长期未作任何补偿与安置；因其做合理抗争，反被对方殴打致残，遂被迫拄着双拐、拖着残疾的身体走上维权诉讼之路，却又因此多次被非法拘禁，遭数次行政拘留和刑事拘留等疯狂打击和报复；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，曾因维权控诉而遭地方当局及其所雇社会闲杂人员非法闯入家中，将其打昏拖走；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年初，曾因抗暴维权惨遭毒打致残，多次上访毫无果效反遭打击报复，致其生活陷入极度困境之中；曾因多次到区政府寻求救助，竟被百般推诿，故在绝望之下，选择跳楼自杀，幸被及时救治，幸免遇难；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年，曾因声援人权律师浦志强案而被丰台区警方殴打，致其右腿韧带损伤，且长时得不到医治；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，曾因向中国人民代表大会谏言，要求对香港《<span lang="EN-US">831</span>决定》进行违宪审查，随遭传唤拘押<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多个小时，并被要求不准再说香港之事；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，曾为免受地方当局暗中迫害，被迫露宿街头，艰难度日；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，因其和同区维权者李美青到中央扫黑除恶督导组驻地反映政府黑社会化强拆问题，而遭到丰台区维稳人员的阻截；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被北京市丰台区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，家被查抄；后又被丰台区检察院以同罪名转正式批捕和起诉，指控其曾因去北京市丰台区政府门口上访、去北京市<span lang="EN-US">999</span>急救中心探望 维权人士曹顺利、在丰台区郑常庄村委会换界选举现场发表相关意见、上网发布有关维权活动信息等等，故而触犯了政府相关法律；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其案在北京市丰台区法院开庭审理；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，终被该法院通过视频方式一审以“寻衅滋事罪”被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日；刑满释放；据悉，看守所关押期间其曾多次被狱中欺凌。此前在北京市天河监狱（北京市大兴区天堂河庆丰路<span lang="EN-US">9</span>号<span lang="EN-US">1290-10</span>信箱，邮编<span lang="EN-US">102609</span>，电话<span lang="EN-US"> 1600628</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，葛志慧又被北京市公安局丰台分局以寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，被关押在北京丰台区看守所。据悉其“寻衅滋事”罪状是将自己历年来被传唤、行拘、刑拘、判刑的判决书等法律文书放到了快手网络上。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/blog-post_86.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/blog-post_86.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> </span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><a name="_Hlk178434750"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2</span></b></a></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178434750;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、高兟</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">高氏兄弟的哥哥。其于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，家人收到三河市公安局的拘留通知书，罪名是涉嫌侵害英雄烈士名誉罪。涉嫌作品为高氏兄弟「高兟<span lang="EN-US">+</span>高强」多年前创作的《枪决基督》、《毛小姐系列》、《下跪忏悔的毛》等雕塑作品。目前，其妻儿遭株连无法出国。高氏兄弟，哥哥高兟生于<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年，弟弟高强生于<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年，二人均为山东济南人。高氏兄弟是中国改革开放时期涌现出的最著名的中国艺术家之一，他们坚定的政治立场在他们的作品中留下了印记。高氏家族在毛泽东发动的文化大革命中遭受灭顶之灾。他们的父亲来自山东沿海省会济南，<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年“文化大革命”最激烈的时候被迫害死亡，兄弟二人当时分别只有<span lang="EN-US">6</span>岁和<span lang="EN-US">12</span>岁。高氏父亲死亡<span lang="EN-US">25</span>天后，母亲和六个孩子才得知父亲所谓“自杀”的消息，他们一直对此表示怀疑。后来，高家来到北京，向中央政府抗议这一不公。最后，他们得到的只是一笔微不足道的赔偿。<span lang="EN-US">1985</span>年起，高氏兄弟一起合作，从事绘画、装置、行为、摄影等艺术活动，尤其是其雕塑和绘画作品，常涉及敏感的政治议题。但高氏兄弟从不认为他们是异议人士，只不过是在从事艺术的过程中表达他们对社会的看法，这可能会触及到当前的中国体制。高氏兄弟是于<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月在北京参加艺术展期间，偶然在方励之给邓小平公开信上签名，由此被当作异议人士，受到当局控制。从<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年到<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年期间，他们一直被禁止出国，直到<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年才被解禁。近年来，习近平当局不断强化对国内异议人士及公共知识分子的言论管控。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，全国人大常委会通过了英雄烈士保护法，旨在追究侮辱诽谤英雄烈士姓名、肖像、名誉等事实的公民的法律责任，并于<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日起实施。高兟就是因为这个罪名被抓捕的。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/blog-post_35.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/blog-post_35.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">3</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、张文鹏：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1993</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">31</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">23</span>岁大学毕业后，张文鹏就考取得律师资格证书，按照中国的法律规定，实习一年就能获得律师执业证书，但是他实习<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年了，一直无法获得执业证。原因是他一直在反对“官办律师协会”，上了司法部的黑名单，因此青岛市司法局一直刁难他，不给他执业证，一拖就是<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。张文鹏被律师界誉为著名实习律师的一条，他揭露律协的腐败，痛斥行贿律师，因此也得罪了一些既得利益者，以至于永久被禁止执业。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年张文鹏在网上发布了实名举报信，指控青岛司法局局长万振东行贿、挥霍公款、渎职等<span lang="EN-US">3</span>大罪责。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，在山东晓临律师事务所实习的张文鹏在微博发文称：<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，他在深圳被青岛市公安局市南分局跨省传唤，他被衣服扒光，内裤都不让穿，持续传唤八小时，理由是扰乱单位秩序。张文鹏到深圳本地派出所询问，了解到，跨省传唤的事由是“曾擅自闯入了青岛司法局”。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，张文鹏又因为代理海韵集团案件，帮助当事人喊冤，被三亚警方以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪予以刑事拘留。就在他被刑事拘留前，该案辩护人北大博士张庆方律师被通知将吊销律师执照。这显然就是三亚警方利用公权对海韵代理人予以打击报复。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/blog-post_27.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/blog-post_27.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">4</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、朱桂芹：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2024</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，辽宁维权人士女士发出求救信息，她被强制送到辽宁省沈阳开原精神病医院。目前还不清楚是什么原因朱桂芹被强制送到精神病院，是谁把她送进去的。朱桂芹算是中国大陆访民的代表人物。<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多年来，反复被拘留、被劳教（劳教尚未废除时）、被判刑。朱桂芹一家兄弟姊妹五人受迫害的遭遇触目惊心，大哥、二姐被迫害致死，姐妹三人被劳教。二哥朱传清，两次被劳教，在劳教所里被打伤致残“脑外伤癫痫”导致朱桂芹为哥哥讨公道，上访十几年没有结果。朱桂芹是为被劳动教养期间打残、精神失常的哥哥伸冤到北京上访。在上访过程中，朱桂芹遭到了和哥哥同样的摧残迫害，<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年被送进辽宁马三家女子劳教所关<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，劳动教养期间被警察打残。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年因与曹顺利（曹顺利北京人权捍卫者，<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被迫害致死，至今无死亡真相）等人一起维权被关押在北京市女子劳教所<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，在这期间经常遭到警察殴打。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日北京两会期间，顺城区信访局人员雇佣无业黑恶人员将朱桂芹押回抚顺市，政府人员关押毒打朱桂芹，导致朱桂芹<span lang="EN-US">6</span>根肋骨被打断。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年，朱桂芹还被辽宁抚顺市顺城区法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/blog-post_24.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/blog-post_24.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">5</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark:
