_Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、白才明：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">四川省凉山州冕宁县基督徒、残障传道人，白才明右手自小残疾<span lang="EN-US">(</span>但可以骑摩托车出去传福音<span lang="EN-US">),</span>平时以捡拾废品为生<span lang="EN-US">,</span>并支撑女儿蒙恩和儿子上学。白才明于<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年就跟随其母亲皈依基督教了<span lang="EN-US">,</span>与妻子董世霞在教会相识<span lang="EN-US">,</span>一直在雅安农村传福音。<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年<span lang="EN-US">,</span>因信徒在白才明家聚会<span lang="EN-US">, </span>白才明被劳动教养两年半。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">白才明持守基督教信仰<span lang="EN-US">,</span>唯独读《圣经》<span lang="EN-US">,</span>没有宗派观<span lang="EN-US">,</span>与其他教会没有联络。大概有十位左右老信徒愿意和，才明、董世霞夫妇一起过信仰生活<span lang="EN-US">,</span>他们并没有给这种聚会形式取个教会名字。由于都是农村老年信徒<span lang="EN-US">,</span>对白才明没有供奉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日<span lang="EN-US">,</span>白才明因所谓的“搞违法基督教活动”被四川省凉山州冕宁县公安局刑事拘留<span lang="EN-US">,</span>罪名是“非法经营罪”，面临被起诉。其妻子董世霞因所谓的不配合被治安拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天<span lang="EN-US">,</span>已于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日回到家中。目前白才明被羁押在冕宁县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/blog-post_22.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/blog-post_22.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">6</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、李旭芳：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">无锡维权人士，家住在江苏省湖滨区湖滨镇大福村山门口<span lang="EN-US">44</span>号。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月李旭芳进京上访，反映周边树木无手续被砍伐报警后警察不但不处理，而且还勾结串通在一起，砍掉更大面积的树木。<a name="_Hlk178436593"><span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月</a><span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被无锡市公安局无锡市经济开发区分局鼋头渚派出所警察抓回原籍，并已被以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，目前关押在无锡女子看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/blog-post_18.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/blog-post_18.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">7</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、张展：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1983</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日出生，陕西省咸阳市人，上海市浦东新区居民，曾任职于上海市某证券公司高管，原执业律师，公民记者，人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。早期，曾就读于西南财经大学金融专业并获取硕士学位；自<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年起，离开家乡到上海谋职；曾为追求自由理想而甘愿放弃在一家证券公司的高薪职位；曾任职律师，但后因在网上发表针砭时弊的文章而遭报复，被迫离开律师岗位；因不满中共当局的政治现状，曾长期在网络平台发表批评“一党专政”、腐败滥权等言论，且因内容尖锐，颇具针对性，而被上海警方多次约谈、传唤及威胁；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年以来，因在微信等社交软件上大量转发香港“反送中”抗议视频及文图资料，尤其是在上海街头举伞要求结束社会主义制度、共产党下台等，随于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被上海市黄浦区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，期间曾被两次做强制性“精神病鉴定”，至<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日才准予取保候审释放；自<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年初以来，曾因武汉冠状病毒疫情蔓延，其为了获取一手数据，不惧风险，亲赴武汉做实地疫情考察与报导；此举很快遭到中共当局的极端不满和迅速打压；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，被武汉警方从一家暂住旅店抓走，次日被上海市浦东新区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，被浦东新区检察院予以批捕；<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，其案被移送至上海市浦东新区法院；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被该法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日；据悉，其家属要求探监曾长期遭拒；其因狱中长期绝食抗议，被强行灌食，致其身体情况十分虚弱。此前张展一直在上海市女子监狱服刑。张展女士<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月刑满出狱<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月后，即<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，张展因营救最近被抓捕的甘肃青年民主活动人士张盼成，从上海只身赴甘肃，说服张母签署了委托书。随后其回到老家陕西咸阳，后与<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日在当地被上海警方带回，后音信全无。家人遭警方警告未予透露张展情况。后本网通过多方信息来源，确认张展女士已遭当局以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，目前关押在浦东看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/8.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/8.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">8</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、覃律：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1969</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日出生，广西壮族自治区梧州市岺溪市人，江苏省镇江市长住居民，网购代理销售者，多个微信群组的组建者和信息发布者，民主维权公民，中国在押政治犯。早年曾因做网购和售卖境外卡，故其利用容易注册微信号之便组建了许多微信群；曾因其为人谦和热心、乐善好施，尤其是在微信群里经常给需要帮助的网友捐助和寄送物品等，而被网友交口称赞；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，因其经常热衷于关注社会不公事件及支持正义行动人士，尤其是每天从境外转发大量的中共禁闻到群里，封号封群又重新申请，故而引起中共江苏省当局的密切关注和维稳打压；后因其听闻一些可能会被当局抓捕的信息，随被迫逃离家乡，东躲西藏，并曾藏倪于深山之中过野人般的生活<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个多月，后到了缅甸，但最终仍被江苏省镇江市警方跨境抓回，其家遭查抄，当场没收白酒<span lang="EN-US">149</span>瓶，帽子<span lang="EN-US">1</span>顶，苹果<span lang="EN-US">PLUS</span>手机<span lang="EN-US">1</span>部；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，被镇江市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”指定居所监视居住；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，又被镇江市警方以同罪名刑事拘留；后被镇江市检察院追加罪名，即涉嫌“偷越国境罪”正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，被江苏省镇江市润州区法院以“寻衅滋事罪”（判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月）和“偷越国境罪”（判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月），数罪并罚，最终执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>元，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。覃律于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日上午被湖南永州市国安联合多个部门，非法上门搜查，并带走拘留。警方曾审问跟境外势力勾结之类的，后来证据不足，最后定非法经营罪，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被刑事拘留。家人向警方交纳<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元的罚款，至今未放人。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/blog-post_5.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/blog-post_5.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><a name="_Hlk178439961"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">9</span></b></a></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178439961;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、华秀珍</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1946</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年生，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年七十八岁，女，上海著名人权捍卫者、疫苗受害家属。因退休金遭当局非法克扣而上访再遭刑事拘留、批捕，狱中病情危重。华秀珍<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年为女儿谭华疫苗受害上访获刑一年两个月，随后被其原单位宁波大学取消了母女俩唯一生活来源养老金，申诉无果。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日华秀珍、谭华母女到浙江省政府上访后均被刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日华秀珍被批捕，七月因严重高血压和房颤等危重病情转入监管医院，至今不认罪不认罚，公安不给家属拘留和批捕通知，看守所扣押家属信件，近况不明。而其女儿谭华被取保候审后，又被非法拘禁在家，六个保安看门，境况艰难。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New lang="EN-US">1965</span>年生。原是农安县合隆镇供电所的正式职工，因坚持法轮功信仰，多次遭中共人员骚扰、抓捕、关押等迫害，并被单位非法开除。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日中午，苏秀福和徐亚芬、尹桂英在农安县合隆镇鑫海明珠小区被长春市公安局、农安县公安局、合隆派出所警察联合抓捕，均被关押在长春市第二看守所。后获悉苏秀福遭德惠市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年。目前被关押在农安县看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2035</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日中午，法轮功学员苏秀福和徐亚芬、尹桂英在农安县合隆镇鑫海明珠小区被长春市公安局、农安县公安局、合隆派出所警察联合抓捕，均被关押在长春市第二看守所。后获悉徐亚芬遭德惠市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。目前被转监到吉林省女子监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2034</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">尹桂英：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">吉林省长春市农安县法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年约七十多岁。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日中午，法轮功学员苏秀福和徐亚芬、尹桂英在农安县合隆镇鑫海明珠小区被长春市公安局、农安县公安局、合隆派出所警察联合抓捕，均被关押在长春市第二看守所。后获悉尹桂英遭德惠市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。目前被转监到吉林省女子监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2034</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/12.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/12.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">4/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杨智渊：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">1990</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日生，台湾社运人士。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年曾加入民主进步党，<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年曾参与创建台湾民族党，该党以“推动台湾成为独立主权国家并加入联合国”为纲领。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年曾经跟随中华统一促进党一同前往上海市，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年创立“国民阵线”，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年支持香港民主派。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，出境前往中国大陆福建省厦门市经商居住，随后超过<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个多月没有回台，故被外界认为其选择留在大陆发展。后报名参加在浙江省温州市举行的围棋比赛，最后于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日在该市被浙江省温州市国家安全局以「涉嫌分裂国家犯罪和煽动分裂国家犯罪」为由刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，中国中央电视台表示，温州市国家安全局已变更杨智渊刑事强制措施，将刑事拘留转为「指定居所监视居住」，于<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日通知其家属，他是继李明哲后，遭中国大陆指定居所监视居住的台湾人。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，陆委会召开记者会声援杨智渊，表示其应无罪，呼吁大陆当局释放其回台。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，杨智渊案由浙江省温州市国家安全局侦查终结，并移送温州市检察院审查起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，温州市中级人民法院判处杨智渊分裂国家罪罪名成立，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: lang="EN-US">29</span>日，长春市净月大街派出所多名警察到吴青元家中抄家，将吴青元和他老伴带到派出所非法关押、审问。吴青元夫妇都已<span lang="EN-US">70</span>多岁，他们身体虚弱、行动不便。警察仍将夫妇二人送至看守所关押。吴青元的老伴因身体检查不合格，被拒收；吴青元被关押在长春市公安监管中心（即长春市看守所）。后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。最后被长春市净月区法院重判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年六十多岁，家住庆阳市西峰区董志镇。她因坚持真、善、忍信仰，经常遭中共官员及警察骚扰，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年她曾被判刑。曹稳梅女士<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月被警察抓捕后，。因当地看守以疫情为由拒收，曹稳梅当时得以回家。但正宁县公安局国保大队构陷当地检察院、法院，对曹稳梅进行司法迫害，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年初被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月获知，曹稳梅已被当地法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: lang="EN-US">2001</span>年她开始修炼法轮功。在中共对法轮功持续至今二十五年的迫害中，周玉祯遭中共看守所、马三家劳教所、监狱酷刑折磨，狱中时间长达十年，被迫害得骨瘦如柴，九死一生。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">山东寿光法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年生，寿光市仙霞服装退休职工，她家住山东省寿光市教授新村。一九九八年开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日上午，寿光市国保及寿光市古城街道派出所警察闯入袁俊花的家，抓捕了她。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，袁俊花被放回家。袁俊花为了躲避迫害，被迫流离失所。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日上午，袁俊花因回家一趟，被警察跟踪，在租住处被寿光警察抓捕。当天下午，袁俊花被关押到潍坊市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，山东省寿光法院第三次对袁俊花开庭，袁俊花被判刑期<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、罚款三万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">重庆市巴南区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1949</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">75</span>岁。段在英老人家住重庆市巴南区花溪街道花溪村。段在英于<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年开始修炼法轮功，自中共一九九九年七月疯狂迫害法轮功后，段在英因坚持法轮功信仰，多次遭到绑架、关押，她曾三次被劳教，三次遭判刑，累计坐牢十二年。段在英于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20 </span>日在巴南界石镇给路人宣讲法轮功时被警察抓捕。虽然当晚得以回家，但八天后的<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，她又被巴南区国保警察抓捕，被关押到界石镇看守所。之后她遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日生，是辽宁知名人权捍卫者林明洁的哥哥。因维权屡遭沈阳当局打压，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年被以寻衅滋事罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被监视居住，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日再次被刑事拘留，同年<span &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张兵</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">山西法轮功学员，男，张兵被曾因发法轮功资料被判刑两年。张兵<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月获悉，张兵、黎洪涛两人均被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。目前已经转监到山西晋中监狱服刑。张兵被关押在山西晋中监狱十监区。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">河北石家庄籍法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1975</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月生，西南交大本科毕业，工程监理工程师。黎洪涛<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年开始修炼法轮功，曾于<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年上北京天安门为法轮功喊冤，回来后，受到迫害，被中铁一局开除公职。<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年，因散发法轮功神韵光盘，被石家庄市警察抓捕迫害，并被判刑四年。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，黎洪涛在打工的汕尾陆河县工地被山西太原警察跨省抓捕，理由是他在微信群发布了所谓“不正当言论”。后黎洪涛被绑架至太原看守所非法关押。同时被绑架的还有山西法轮功学员张兵，据悉他<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年在微信群里发了一首法轮功歌曲而被抓捕。近悉，黎洪涛、张兵已经被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被转监至山西晋中监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">59</span>岁。大学毕业，兰州市七里河区八里窑镇卫生院退休医生。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，她在兰州小西湖公园宣讲法轮功，被学生举报，随后她被小西湖派出所、七里河国保大队抓捕、抄家。刘桂芳被关押在兰州市第一看守所，后遭批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日早，兰州市城关区法院庭审刘桂芳，刘桂芳本人和律师都作了无罪辩护。后刘桂芳被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月，提出上诉，二审于维持原判，后刘桂芳被转监到兰州九州女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/34.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><a name="_Hlk178429085"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178429085;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘让芳</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">黑龙江省宝清县法轮功学员，女，居住双鸭山市宝清县<span lang="EN-US">852</span>农场一分厂七队，原本是农场小学教师，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年已经<span lang="EN-US">70</span>多岁。一九九九年七月中共江泽民集团迫害法轮功以后，因坚修法轮功，刘让芳女士被抓捕九次，曾被关押到洗脑班迫害半年，被劳教两年，在佳木斯西格木劳教所遭受了非人的折磨：强迫坐铁椅子折磨七天、关禁闭室、奴役、野蛮灌食等；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被抓捕、后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，在黑龙江女子监狱遭受了毒打、坐小板凳、码坐、奴役等种种折磨。刘让芳<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月在当地<span lang="EN-US">852</span>农场超市法轮功相资料时被抓捕，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，她才结束三年牢狱，刚出来时靠拐棍走。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，刘让芳又被抓捕，被关押在黑龙江省双鸭山市看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日在红兴隆法院被开庭；是黑龙江省建三江法院的人到红兴隆法院所谓“审判”，当日没宣判。后获悉，其被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">58</span>岁，汉族，家住湘西土家族苗族自治州花垣县峨碧村。她因坚持真、善、忍信仰、坚持把法轮大法的真相告诉乡邻，而遭中共的残酷迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，肖永康在卖菜时，给一老人讲法轮功，被跟踪的便衣发现，叫来三角岩派出所警察，对她拳打脚踢，强行拖走，把她关押到湘西州看守所。后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。花垣县法院分别于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日法庭审肖永康。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，花垣县法院对肖永康判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金一万元。她被关押在湘西自治州看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">山东省临沂市沂水县法轮功学员，女，早年修炼法轮功，多次被中共绑架、关押。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，李孝梅在沂水县马站大集传播法轮功时，遭抓捕、抄家，后被批捕。在被劫往临沂看守所关押时，她因体检不合格被看守所拒收。<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，李孝梅被“取保候审”回家。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，李孝梅被沙沟派出所警察抓捕，之后，沂南县法院对她判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。因身体原因，监外执行。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被沂水县公安局入室抓捕收监。近日获悉：李孝梅被关押到山东省女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年底去北京为法轮功上访遭抓捕、关入北镇拘留所、看守所。在看守所时，李宝辉遭受了多种酷刑迫害如；十冬腊月天被脱光衣服往身上浇凉水以及拳打脚踢、罚蹲、罚站等。后李宝辉被劳教三年、关入锦州教养院折磨。李宝辉<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日在家被北镇市公安国保警察抓捕，后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，现在被关押在锦州市监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月左右被凌海法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，随后被转监到辽宁省女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日西藏抗暴纪念日当天发布敏感信息。向巴曲培巴曲培先被关押在位于热贡的监狱。后转监至西宁市的监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月份向巴曲培被中共当局判处<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，在兰州市安宁区租住处，马祖福被警察抓捕。后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，马祖福被当地法院庭审，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年六十四岁。家住北京市朝阳区三源里南小街，原在保险公司工作。<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年开始修炼法轮功。后遭中共当局多次迫害。陈淑平女士<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月突然失联，处于强迫失踪状态。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月获悉，陈淑平被当地法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">为了更方便人们查询本网统计的在押政治犯、良心犯的名单，本网每期随《中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告》一起发布《中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯名单索引》。本索引将本期报告所统计的人员名单，以人员姓名拼音字母排序（<span lang="EN-US">A</span>、<span lang="EN-US">B</span>、<span lang="EN-US">C</span>、<span lang="EN-US">D</span>、<span lang="EN-US">E</span>、<span lang="EN-US">F.....X</span>、<span lang="EN-US">Y</span>、<span lang="EN-US">Z</span>）。查询者可依据姓名的第一个拼音字母，即可查询到相关人员姓名，而其简介均可在报告中查找到。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk55009291;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">如您获知有未上名单的政治犯良心犯的境况，请随时向我们知会，<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">联系邮箱：<span lang="EN-US">wqw2011@gmail.com<o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk55009291;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">名单索引如下<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span
